            <h3 class="j-e-title" itemprop="headline">

            <div class="j-e-text" itemprop="text">

             <br/>

           OPI: Ate Berries in the Canaries.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <img src="http://img.makeupalley.com/4/5/1/4/1715626.JPG"/>

           <div class="j-c-head-inner">
            <h5 class="j-c-subject" itemprop="name">
             I used to be
            </h5>
            <div class="j-c-poster" itemprop="creator">
             <span class="ljuser i-ljuser i-ljuser-type-P " lj:user="jazzypom">
              <a class="i-ljuser-profile" href="http://jazzypom.livejournal.com/profile" target="_self">
               <img class="i-ljuser-userhead" src="http://l-stat.livejournal.net/img/user_ontd.gif?v=128.7"/>
